* Docs

+ [[https://ipython.readthedocs.io/en/stable/config/options/kernel.html][ipykernel options]]


* Notes

** Pyenv Setup

Create the direnv files necessary to create a new =pyenv venv= under...

Then in the new =venv=, run:

#+begin_src sh
pip install ipykernel numpy
python -m ipykernel install --user --name="emacs-ipykernel"
#+end_src


** Babel Setup



** Misc

*** Opening new blocks

Starts to open the block, but doesn't actually open it.

Shows =Need a valid session and a kernel to form a key=

** Features

Misc

#+BEGIN_SRC emacs-lisp
;; override src lang
(org-babel-jupyter-override-src-block "python")

;; prevent async
(setq ob-async-no-async-languages-alist '("jupyter-python" "jupyter-julia"))
#+END_SRC

*** Media

#+BEGIN_SRC jupyter-python :session py :display plain
import pandas as pd
data = [[1, 2], [3, 4]]
pd.DataFrame(data, columns=["Foo", "Bar"])
#+END_SRC

**** For =k3d=

if local

#+begin_src jupyter-python :results output file link :file (format "%s.html" (dc/org-roam-get-slug))
with open('img/jupyter-k3d.html','w') as fp:
    fp.write(plot.get_snapshot())
#+end_src

write to a file in the volume ... this doesn't work

#+headers: :var jphtml=(format "%s/index.html" jpdir)
#+begin_src jupyter-python :results output link :file jphtml
# the raw vars don't work either

# + PROPERTY: header-args+ :var jpvol=(setq-local jpvol "/nb")
# + PROPERTY: header-args+ :var jpdir=(setq-local jpdir (expand-file-name (dc/org-roam-get-slug) jpvol))

# or if local: :file (expand-file-name (format "%s_k3d.html" (dc/org-roam-get-slug)) jpvol)
with open(jphtml,'w') as fp:
    fp.write(plot.get_snapshot())
print(jphtml)
#+end_src

if handled entirely outside of emacs, it does

#+header: :var jphtml=(format "%s/index.html" jpdir)
#+begin_src jupyter-python
# only static files (no time to figure it out)
with open("fdsa.html",'w') as fp:
    fp.write(plot.get_snapshot())
#+end_src

machine" is confusing. there are many of them with babel generally. probably
better ways to resolve. skills issues? idk
